msg:My family and I recently stayed at Andaz Shenzhen Bay Hotel for one night, and it was truly one of the best hotel experiences we've had with our two young daughters. From the moment we arrived, we were impressed by the warm welcome and exceptional service provided by the staff.

The hotel itself is modern, stylish, and very well-maintained. Our room was spacious, comfortable, and beautifully designed with stunning views of the city skyline. We were especially impressed by the thoughtful touches, such as the complimentary snacks and drinks in the minibar and the personalized welcome note from the hotel manager.

One of the highlights of our stay was the hotel's fantastic amenities. We spent several hours at the hot spa jacuzzi. 

In addition to the amenities, we also appreciated the hotel's convenient location. It's located in a vibrant neighborhood with plenty of shops, restaurants, and attractions nearby. We were able to easily explore the area, and the hotel staff provided us with excellent recommendations for family-friendly activities.

Overall, our stay at Andaz Shenzhen Bay Hotel exceeded our expectations in every way. The hotel is beautiful, the service is exceptional, and the amenities are top-notch. We would highly recommend this hotel to anyone looking for a luxurious and family-friendly stay in Shenzhen.

posted:Posted October 8, 2021
msg:Great option for a staycation.

Booked the panoramic view room for two nights over the October national holiday. Like other Andaz properties, the decor was unique but still tasteful. No loud guests and no unaccounted for children running around. All the staff (concierge, dining, housekeeping) were extremely friendly, professional, and helpful. 

The room was clean and had all the amenities you can think of. The layout also made sense, no weird furniture placement. The minibar was stocked with local drinks and a good variety of snacks and there were many options for room service.

The gym was clean, routinely sanitized, and the stationary machines were nicely spaced. There were also a set of free weights and kettlebells. If you want a space for yoga, there‚Äôs a sectioned off room in the middle as well.

Buffet breakfast is in the East restaurant space and provided the typical options along with a menu to order from.

Not much to do around the area except the new Talent Park (has an exhibition hall) and the new Shenzhen Bay MixC mall that mainly has luxury brands (Goyard, Harry Winston, Loewe etc). If you‚Äôre willing to walk, about 20 minutes away is Coastal City for affordable shopping and food options. The closest subway station is Houhai with access to the 11 and 2/8 lines.

Andaz Shenzhen Bay is perfect for those wanting to get away from the hustle and bustle of Futian/Nanshan.

This trip was for my wife and I to celebrate our birthday. When we booked the hotel, we informed the hotel that the room would be decorated and a cake would be delivered. He also created Andaz Tokyo, Mandarin Oriental Guangzhou, and Rosewood Hotel in London. s work.
The master insists on one city at a time, with a very personal style. Photos cannot capture the gleaming textures, such as wood, leather, wallpaper, fences, marble...
I was particularly surprised and liked the design of the entrance of Andaz. It is very low-key and simple. People passing by have no idea that there is such a beautiful hotel inside, but as soon as it opens, it is a paradise and a paradise. Walking through the Hall of Fame, people with dreams in their hearts will probably have some kind of secret passion.
In addition to the hotel's hardware facilities and catering products that are commendable, the staff's service is also experienced in details. Guest relations Hana guided us to the guest room, and guest relations assistant manager Pany introduced the hotel's various facilities and time arrangements, which was far warmer than putting a guest book in the room. Seeing that we brought children, they upgraded the room type for us for free, gave us an extra bed, and gave us a bottle of red wine. Before leaving today for the Chinese New Year, we also gave the children a picture book and a bear doll with the Andaz logo.
Andaz Shenzhen is one of the few hotels I have stayed in that I would like to stay again. Thanks again to Assistant Guest Relations Manager Pany and Guest Relations Hany for their enthusiastic help.

The room layout is exquisite, modern luxury and comfortable, a bit like Park Hyatt
The scenery outside the window is beautiful, capturing the "most beautiful Shenzhen Bay" landscape...

The Hyatt management team is trustworthy. Andy, the front desk manager, helped me arrange the 16th room on the floor that the children liked. Another Miss Zhang at the front desk provided the children with welcome tea and snacks...

After checking in, I immediately discovered some problems: 1. The swimming pool is not big, but it accommodates nearly 20 children and 10 adults at the same time. Although the on-site staff Xiao Zhang Xiaolai is diligent and conscientious, it is obvious that the unlimited number of people will be more difficult. There is a big security risk, it is suitable to adopt the reservation system like Mandarin Oriental to control the number of people; 2. The swimming pool locker room does not restrict the use of other people's mobile phones, and there is an obvious risk of privacy leakage; Friendliness etc...

In the afternoon, I met Concierge Specialist Kelly Liu during the drink reception event. She asked me about the check-in experience in detail. After she reported the above problems to her, she received a positive call back after she gave feedback to the management. She went to the swimming pool and the locker room the next day. Compared with the previous day, you will find that it has been significantly improved... The hotel is managed in the process, and the service is very strong... The beauty Liu Qiuting is conscientious and responsible, worthy of praiseüëçüëç

The room is not only quiet, it is very comfortable to live in, and the free drinks/snacks in the room are obviously better than other homes...

The overall hotel is very good and strong. The weak link is in the breakfast cafeteria. The layout is narrow, the layout is scattered, there are few choices, and it is obviously inconsistent with the standards of hotels of the same level. Fortunately, the things made are not bad; although the sauna room is very good, it is a pity that there is no equipment to use. The worst part is the housing deposit. It is not refunded immediately like other hotels, but it is delayed until I leave the next hotel and receive the deposit refunded there. It has obviously exceeded the promised 24 hours, so I had to ask Ctrip customer service to follow up. just received...

If it weren't for the hotel's Andy Kelly Liu, Xiao Zhang, Xiao Lai and many other unknown staff members who made me so satisfied, and the children were reluctant to leave, I would definitely deduct points...

Hope to have a "perfect" experience next time you stay...

At the beginning of the lanterns, the drooping eyes are the clearness and clarity of the wind curtain and green curtain of the talent park, which makes people yearn for it. The passing roads and overpasses build the skeleton and blood of the city, and towering buildings are seen everywhere, one after another, one after another, building a patchwork of iron and steel forests, like delicate silver buckles. On the black and green cloak adorned in the wilderness, it shone day and night. I saw the lights of thousands of homes again, the broken light floating on the glass window lattice, the continuous flow on the road, and the lights of the cars were interspersed together, extending to the distance, becoming a slowly flowing galaxy.

The sleep experience is quite satisfactory and unremarkable, like a calm lake, gently submerging what you want

Although the breakfast is not as good as Bazhen Jade Food and Phoenix Marrow and Dragon Liver, it is indeed delicious and delicious. There is a wide variety of food, and when you pick up a piece of tender and delicious green vegetables or a piece of chicken in a sauce from the Chinese dining area, your eyes will light up. Put a few handfuls of raw vegetables and sweet fruits from the western dining area on a porcelain plate, a few spoonfuls of salad dressing salt fall on the surface of the vegetables like snow, and then add a few slices of smoked salmon, the fish is plump, fresh fish and refreshing vegetables are the best A good match is to use fried mushrooms and garnished with delicious bread. The refreshing taste of the dish is blended with the mellowness of the fish. The fresh and mellow delicacy overflows the lips and teeth, just like the elegant and bright scenery outside the window. What I like most is not the jade plate under the light, but the inconspicuous raspberry tower in the corner. When I take a bite, the tip of my tongue touches the crispy, burnt-yellow dough, and then it breaks through the soft wall. The pulp is crushed, and the sweet and sour of the pulp fills the mouth immediately, splashing like fireworks to stimulate the taste buds, the tongue is dyed with bright red juice, the sourness is past the sweet taste of melons and fruits in summer, the sweet fragrance of whipped cream is not Greasy, the butter cake is crispy and lingering, holding up the cucumber juice and chatting, feasting on the delicious food on the plate, when the bowls and chopsticks collide, the footsteps of the new year are already approaching
